                             <div class="elementor-post__text" style="width: auto;display:none;" id="integrate37412"> 
                              <h3 class="elementor-post__title"> <a style="color: #282f38 !important;" target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://aiw217.saas.contentserv.com/admin/rest/smart/preset/95?ContextIDs=11857">Contentserv</a> </h3> 
                              <div class="elementor-post__excerpt">
                                The Matomo Connector developed by Contentserv Business Solutions allows to place Matomo embed codes in typical Contentserv PIM scenarios. This allows to track many important usages like media downloads, search requests or PIM and DAM statistics. Also various interactions like REST service request can be tracked through the Matomo Tracking API. 
                              </div>

              <div class="elementor-row"> 
               <div class="elementor-column elementor-col-100 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-bc10c37" data-id="bc10c37" data-element_type="column">

                 <div class="elementor-widget-wrap"> 
                  <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-01ec9ed elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="01ec9ed" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"> 
                   <div class="elementor-widget-container"> 
                    <div class="elementor-text-editor elementor-clearfix"> 
                     <p>Please note that these plugins, addons and modules linked to on this page are built by third party developers NOT members of the Matomo team. The source code has not been reviewed by the core team, nor did we test them ourselves. Therefore, please use these with caution and report any issues you may experience to the original developer. Keeping the list up to date</p>
                     <p>To report a broken link, or to submit a new plugin <a href="mailto:hello@matomo.org">please get in touch</a>. See also the guide <a href="https://matomo.org/integrate/how-to/">Best practises for Integration Plugins</a>.</p>
